 var width_window = $(window).width();
 var my_device = 'pc';
 if(/Windows Phone/i.test(navigator.userAgent)){
 
 	my_device = "tablet" ;
 	if(width_window <= MIN_WIDTH_DESKTOP_SIZE)
 	{
    		my_device = "mobile" ;
    	}
    	else if(width_window > MIN_WIDTH_DESKTOP_SIZE && width_window < 685)
    	{
    		my_device = "tablet_7" ;
    	}
 }
 else if(/Android/i.test(navigator.userAgent)){
 	
 	my_device = "tablet" ;
 	if(width_window <= MIN_WIDTH_DESKTOP_SIZE)
 	{
    		my_device = "mobile" ;
    	}
    	else if(width_window > MIN_WIDTH_DESKTOP_SIZE && width_window < 685)
    	{
    		my_device = "tablet_7" ;
    	}
 }
 else if(/iPhone|iPad|iPod/i.test(navigator.userAgent)){
 	
 	my_device = "tablet" ;
 	if(width_window <= MIN_WIDTH_DESKTOP_SIZE)
 	{
    		my_device = "mobile" ;
    	}
    	else if(width_window > MIN_WIDTH_DESKTOP_SIZE && width_window < 685)
    	{
    		my_device = "tablet_7" ;
    	}
 
 }
 else if(/Macintosh/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
     my_device = 'pc';
 }
 
 $(document).ready(function() {
 	calculatePadding();
 	if(my_device == "pc")
 	{
 		//console.log(MIN_WIDTH_WINDOW+" "+min_width_window);
 		//$('fieldset.wrapper-content-V2').css('min-width', MIN_WIDTH_WINDOW+"px"); // fixed min-width
 	}
 	else if(my_device == "mobile")
 	{
 		$('fieldset.wrapper-content-V2').css('min-width', "320px");
 	}
 
 	if(current_store == "buffet")
 	{	
 		$('#tab_buffet').attr('id','tab_buffet_current');
 		$('#tab_ebook').attr('id','tab_ebook');
 		if(jMeb.empty(expire_date))
 		{
 			$.ajax({
 	        type: "POST",
 			url: "Ajax.php?action=userGetBundleTypeItemByBundleType",
 			data: ({
 				bundle_type : bundle_type ,
 			}), 
 			success: function(res) 
 	        {
 				try
 	            {
 					var result = jQuery.parseJSON(res);
 	                if(result.status.success == false)
 	                {
 	                	return false;
 	                }
 	                else
 	                {	
 	                	if(jMeb.empty(result['data']['bundle_type_item_list']))
 	                	{
 	                		disable_bundle = true;
 	                		changeBundleButtonListingToSubscribe(disable_bundle);
 							//changeBundleButtonViewBookListingToSubscribe(disable_bundle);
 	                	}
 	                	else
 	                	{
 	                		disable_bundle = false;
 	                		changeBundleButtonListingToSubscribe(disable_bundle);
 							//changeBundleButtonViewBookListingToSubscribe(disable_bundle);
 	                	}
 	                }	
 				}
 	            catch(err)
 	            {
 	                mebUnblockUI();
 				}
 	        }
 	   		});
 		}
 		
 		$('#tab_buffet').attr('id','tab_buffet_current');
 		$('#tab_ebook').attr('id','tab_ebook');
 	}
 
 
 	document.onclick = function(event){
 	    //$('#hide_menu_publisher').hide(); 
 	    var list_hide_profile_publisher = $('#hide_profile_publisher').css('display');
 		var hide_search_publisher = $('#hide_search_publisher').css('display');
 	    
 	    if(list_hide_profile_publisher != "none" || hide_search_publisher != "none" )
 	    {
 		    var hasParent = false;
 		    for(var node = event.target; node != document.body; node = node.parentNode)
 		    {
 		    	if(node.id == 'list-menu-vertical' || node.id == 'hide_profile_publisher' || node.id == 'menu_right_v2')
 		    	{
 		            hasParent = true;
 		            break;
 	        	}
 	        }
 
 	        if(hasParent == false)
 	        {
 				hideToggleMenu();
 	        	hideAllTopMenu();
 	        }
 	    }
 	}

 // ตัวแปล id_index จะถูกสร้างขึ้นมาใหม่ ทุกครั้งที่มีการ Resize จึงต้องถูก clearTimeout ไป จนกระทั่งสิ้นสุดการ Resize จะใช้ id_index ตัวสุดท้ายมาคิด
 // ดังนั้น ชื่อตัวแปล จึงห้ามมีซ้ำกัน ในแต่ละหน้า (จึงใช้ชื่อ file เป็นตัวตั้งชื่อ)
 var id_index; 
 $(window).resize(function() {
     clearTimeout(id_index);
     id_index = setTimeout(function(){ 
     	calculatePadding();
 
     	var width_document = getWidthDocument();
     	$('#bg-store-menubar-horizontal').css('width',width_document);
     	$('div#bg_head_v2').css('width',width_document);
     }, 300);
     
 });

 	function checkDeviceStateHome(){
 	    var width_window = getWidthWindow();
 	    if(width_window > 860 && device_state == "mobile")
 	    {
 	        showHomeBanner();
 	        device_state = "web";
 	    }
 	    else if(width_window < 860 && device_state == "web")
 	    {
 	        showHomeBannerMobile();
 	        device_state = "mobile";
 	    }
 	    
 	    //calculateMargin('fieldset.book_listing_v2');
  		calculateMargin('fieldset.category_group_listing');
 	    
 	    if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined" &&  getCookie('user_token') != '') 
 	    {
 	        changeButton();
 	    }
 	}

 	function getCategoriesPage(){
 
 		/*$cache = new Store(array("token"=>Cookie::get("officer_token"), "category"=>"0"));
 		$result_json = $cache->getCategoriesPage();
 		$result_arr = Response::decode_json($result_json);
 
 		html += '<fieldset class="listing">';
 		//$data = $_result1['data'];
 		System::loadClass('Security');
 
 		Response::getHeadText('head-category', '', 'Meb Special Collection', 'img_head_blue_book');
 		$cache = $result_arr['category_group'];
 		if(is_array($cache) && count($cache) > 0)
 		{
 			System::loadClass('Security');
 			//Response::getCategoryListing($cache);
 			Response::getCategoryGroupListingHome($cache);
 		}*/
 
 		var token = '';
 		$.ajax({
 			type: "POST",
 			url: "Ajax.php?action=CallWrapper",
 			data: ({
 		            api_call : 'Store',
 		            method_call : 'getCategoriesPage',
 					token : 'token',
 					category : 0,
 			}),
 			success: function(res) {
 				var result = jQuery.parseJSON(res);
 				if(result.status.success == false)
 				{	
 				
 				}
 				else if(!jMeb.empty(result['category_group']))
 				{
 					var html = '';
 					var width_window = getWidthWindow();
 					if(width_window > MIN_WIDTH_DESKTOP_SIZE)
 					{
 						html += '<fieldset  class="content-details-V2">';
 							html += getHeadTextV2(translateLocale('meb_special_collection','Meb&nbsp;Special&nbsp;Collection'), true);
 							html += getCategoryGroupListingHome(result['category_group']);		
 						html += '</fieldset>';		
 					}
 	                $('#category_group_listing_home').html(html);
 
 	                calculateMargin('fieldset.category_group_listing');
 	                calculatePadding();
 				}
 				
 			}
 		});
 	}

         <div id="tagcloud" style="padding:5px;font-weight:normal;text-align:center;font-family:Kanit, tahoma, thonburi;border: 1px solid #B1CB35;border-radius: 5px;">

        <script>
         var keyword_obj;
 $.fn.tagcloud.defaults = {
     size: {start: 16, end: 24, unit: 'px'},
     color: {start: '#B1CB35', end: '#FF0000'}
 };
     
 $(document).ready(function(){
     setHeadText()
     getSearchKeywordCache();
 });
 
 function setHeadText()
 {
     var html = getHeadTextV2('Top Search');
     $("#tagcloud").before(html);
 }
 
 function getSearchKeywordCache()
 {
     jQuery.ajax({
   		type: "Post",
   		url: "Ajax.php?action=CallWrapper",
   		data: ({
             api_call : 'Store',
             method_call : 'userGetSearchKeywordCache',
             page_no : 1,
             app_id : DEFAULT_APP_ID,
             app_platform : APP_PLATFORM,
             result_per_page : 80
         }),
         success: function(res){	  
             try
             {
                 var result = jQuery.parseJSON(res);
                 if(result.status.success == true)
                 {
                     keyword_obj = result['data']['search'];
                     var html = getHtmlTagCloud();
                     jQuery('#tagcloud').html(html);
                     runTagcloud();
                 }
             }
             catch (err){}
         }
     });
 }
 
 function getHtmlTagCloud()
 {
     var count = 0;
     var keyword_shuffle = [];
     for(var i in keyword_obj)
     {
         if(count == 50)
         {
             break;
         }
         keyword_shuffle[count] = keyword_obj[i];
         count++;
     }
     shuffle(keyword_shuffle);
     
     var html = '';
     for(var i in keyword_shuffle)
     {
         html += '<span class="decoration-none" rel="'+keyword_shuffle[i]['rank']+'">'+keyword_shuffle[i]['search_keyword']+' </span>';
     }
     
     return html;
 }
 
 function runTagcloud()
 {
     $('#tagcloud span').tagcloud();
 }
